16/05/2020, 14:14 - Chary: TGA is a powerful and robust technique to explore the thermal stability of a material. By accurately monitoring the weight of a sample while heating at a constant rate, we can measure changes in a sample’s weight and attribute this to a specific material response to a thermal stress (Figure 1). This is perfect for exploring, in detail, decomposition temperatures and ensuring a material performs adequately in a given temperature range.
16/05/2020, 14:14 - Maneesh: Andi ra idi
16/05/2020, 14:14 - Chary: DSC is a flexible technique to explore thermal transitions within a given sample. By heating a sample and measuring the heat flow as compared to a reference standard, we can access thermoanalytical information on a given material. DSC curves are generated by plotting heat flow (mW) vs sample temperature (°C),
16/05/2020, 14:14 - Chary: DTA is a similar technique to DSC, however instead of measuring the heat flow between the furnace temperature and the sample, you measure the temperature difference between a sample and a standard reference using thermocouples

02/06/2021, 20:41 - Maneesh: When a conductor is placed in a changing magnetic field, the electrons in the conductor move, generating an electric current. Magnets produce such magnetic fields and can be used in various configurations to generate electricity. Depending on the kind of magnet used, a rotating electric generator can have magnets placed in different locations and can generate electricity in different ways. Most of the electricity in use comes from generators that use magnetic fields to produce that electricity.
02/06/2021, 20:42 - Maneesh: These generators are made up of coils of wire that are either rotated through magnetic fields or are stationary around a shaft with rotating magnets. In either case, the coils of wire are exposed to changing magnetic fields created by the magnets.

The magnets can be permanent or electric magnets. Permanent magnets are mainly used in small generators, and they have the advantage that they don't need a power supply. Electric magnets are iron or steel wound with wire. When electricity passes through the wire, the metal becomes magnetic and creates a magnetic field.
02/06/2021, 20:42 - Maneesh: The coils of wire of the generators are conductors, and when the electrons in the wires are exposed to changing magnetic fields, they move, creating an electric current in the wires. The wires are connected together, and the electricity eventually leaves the power station and goes on to power homes and factories.

28/10/2021, 11:37 - Chary: #include <TinyGPS.h>

TinyGPS gps;  //Creates a new instance of the TinyGPS object


void setup()
{
  Serial.begin(9600);  
  Serial.print("Simple TinyGPS library v. "); Serial.println(TinyGPS::library_version());
  Serial.println("Testing GPS");
  Serial.println("Designed by: www.TheEngineeringProjects.com");
  Serial.println();
}

void loop()
{
  bool newData = false;
  unsigned long chars;
  unsigned short sentences, failed;

  // For one second we parse GPS data and report some key values
  for (unsigned long start = millis(); millis() - start < 1000;)
  {
    while (Serial.available())
    {
      char c = Serial.read();
      //Serial.print(c);
      if (gps.encode(c)) 
        newData = true;  
    }
  }

  if (newData)      //If newData is true
  {
    float flat, flon;
    unsigned long age;
    gps.f_get_position(&flat, &flon, &age);   
    Serial.print("Latitude = ");
    Serial.print(flat == TinyGPS::GPS_INVALID_F_ANGLE ? 0.0 : flat, 6);
    Serial.print(" Longitude = ");
    Serial.print(flon == TinyGPS::GPS_INVALID_F_ANGLE ? 0.0 : flon, 6);

  }
 
  Serial.println(failed);
 // if (chars == 0)
   // Serial.println("** No characters received from GPS: check wiring **");
}

06/12/2021, 16:27 - Maneesh: Deaths due to traffic and due to delay of ambulance.
Concept: A mechanical bird where we use the concept of drone will help the humans from death due to traffic and delay of ambulance. When there is an emergency for a person like if a person hit with an accident then the ambulance will reach the destination and save the life. 
But what if there is traffic in the middle of the route?
As the person hit with an accident then the ambulance will get the call from the destination so the call is tracked after this simultaneously there will be the bird will reach the destination before the arrival of ambulance. So that with the help of the bird the traffic will be cleared, before the drone start there will be a signal along with traffic lights in the  junction, then this signal will be activated so that the traffic near the junction will also be cleared simultaneously.
By this method we can minimize the accidents and save the life’s of

Dear Editor,

I am writing to submit my "Voice Command Robot: A Novel Approach for Human-Robot Interaction" research paper for consideration and potential publication in Junikhyat Journal. I firmly believe that this paper aligns perfectly with the scope and objectives of your esteemed journal. Please find attached all the necessary documents related to the submission.

The research presented in this paper represents a significant advancement in the field of robotics, specifically focusing on human-robot interaction through voice commands. This study aimed to develop a novel approach for enabling seamless communication and control between humans and robots using voice commands.

The key contributions and highlights of this research paper are as follows:

1. Abstract: A concise summary of the research objectives, methodology, key findings, and implications.
2. Introduction: An overview of the significance of human-robot interaction and the need for effective voice command systems.
3. Methodology: A detailed description of the design, development, and implementation of the voice command robot, including hardware and software aspects.
4. Results: Presentation and analysis of the performance and accuracy of the voice command recognition system, supported by relevant figures and tables.
5. Discussion: interpretation of the results, comparison with existing voice command systems, and a discussion on the potential applications and impact of the proposed approach.
6. Conclusion: A summary of the key findings, their significance in the field, and avenues for future research and improvements.

This research paper showcases the successful implementation and evaluation of the voice command robot, highlighting its potential for various applications such as assistive robotics, smart homes, and industrial automation. The results demonstrate improved accuracy, response time, and user experience compared to existing voice command systems.

I kindly request you to consider my research paper for publication in Junikhyat Journal. I am confident that this paper will contribute significantly to the knowledge base and inspire further research in the field of human-robot interaction.

Thank you for considering my research paper for publication in Junikhyat Journal. I sincerely appreciate your time and consideration.

Sincerely,
Banka Maneesh
Vignana Bharathi Institute of Technology
